[San Pedro de Urabá - Wikipedia]
San Pedro de Urabá (Spanish pronunciation: [sam ˈpeðɾo ðe wɾaˈβa]) is a municipality in Antioquia Department, Colombia. It is part of the Urabá Antioquia sub-region. San Pedro de Urabá has a tropical monsoon climate (Am) with moderate to little rainfall from December to March and ...
URL: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/San_Pedro_de_Urab%C3%A1

[San Pedro de Uraba (definition and history)]
"Urabá" refers to the Urabá region, a significant geographical and cultural area in northwestern Colombia, known for its tropical climate and diverse ecosystems. The municipality's name, therefore, signifies its patron saint and its location within the broader Urabá territory. San Pedro de Urabá is situated in the department of Antioquia, a region characterized by its mountainous terrain and vibrant culture.
URL: https://www.wisdomlib.org/cities/san-pedro-de-uraba-16179

[Grokipedia: San Pedro de Urabá]

[Urabá Antioquia - Wikipedia]
Urabá Antioquia is a region of Colombia's Antioquia Department that consists of two non-contiguous sections, one forming the northwest of the department, the other the west. Both are along the Atrato River. They are separated by the El Carmen del Darién and Riosucio municipalities of Chocó Department, with territories in both municipalities in dispute with Chocó.
URL: https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Urab%C3%A1_Antioquia

--- [Urabá Antioquia - Wikipedia] ---
Urabá Antioquia is a region of Colombia's Antioquia Department that consists of two non-contiguous sections, one forming the northwest of the department, the other the west. Both are along the Atrato River. They are separated by the El Carmen del Darién and Riosucio municipalities of Chocó Department, with territories in both municipalities in dispute with Chocó. The region is made up by 11 municipalities. Most of this region's northern portion is part of the Colombian Caribbean Region bordering the Caribbean Sea.
